\DoxyCodeLine{00052\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ There\ are\ several\ closely\ related\ types,\ with\ the\ following\ naming}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00053\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ convention:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00054\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \_Tp:\ vectorizable\ (arithmetic)\ type\ (or\ any\ type)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00055\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \_TV:\ \_\_vector\_type\_t<\_Tp,\ \_Np>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00056\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \_TW:\ \_SimdWrapper<\_Tp,\ \_Np>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00057\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \_TI:\ \_\_intrinsic\_type\_t<\_Tp,\ \_Np>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00058\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \_TVT:\ \_VectorTraits<\_TV>\ or\ \_VectorTraits<\_TW>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00059\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ If\ one\ additional\ type\ is\ needed\ use\ \_U\ instead\ of\ \_T.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00060\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Otherwise\ use\ \_T\(\backslash\)d,\ \_TV\(\backslash\)d,\ \_TW\(\backslash\)d,\ TI\(\backslash\)d,\ \_TVT\(\backslash\)d.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00061\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00062\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ More\ naming\ conventions:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00063\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \_Ap\ or\ \_Abi:\ An\ ABI\ tag\ from\ the\ simd\_abi\ namespace}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00064\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \_Ip:\ often\ used\ for\ integer\ types\ with\ sizeof(\_Ip)\ ==\ sizeof(\_Tp),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00065\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \_IV,\ \_IW\ as\ for\ \_TV,\ \_TW}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00066\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \_Np:\ number\ of\ elements\ (not\ bytes)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00067\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \_Bytes:\ number\ of\ bytes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00068\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00069\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Variable\ names:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00070\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \_\_k:\ mask\ object\ (vector-\/\ or\ bitmask)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00071\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00072\ \_GLIBCXX\_SIMD\_BEGIN\_NAMESPACE}
\DoxyCodeLine{00073\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{00094\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ There\ are\ two\ major\ ABIs\ that\ appear\ on\ different\ architectures.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00095\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Both\ have\ non-\/boolean\ values\ packed\ into\ an\ N\ Byte\ register}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00096\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/>\ \#elements\ =\ N\ /\ sizeof(T)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00097\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Masks\ differ:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00098\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ 1.\ Use\ value\ vector\ registers\ for\ masks\ (all\ 0\ or\ all\ 1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00099\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ 2.\ Use\ bitmasks\ (mask\ registers)\ with\ one\ bit\ per\ value\ in\ the\ corresponding}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00100\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ value\ vector}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00101\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00102\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Both\ can\ be\ partially\ used,\ masking\ off\ the\ rest\ when\ doing\ horizontal}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00103\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ operations\ or\ operations\ that\ can\ trap\ (e.g.\ FP\_INVALID\ or\ integer\ division}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00104\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ by\ 0).\ This\ is\ encoded\ as\ the\ number\ of\ used\ bytes.}}
